**STATISTICAL SUPPLEMENT** Pakistan Economic Survey 2019-20 

Economic Adviser’s Wing, Finance Division, Government of Pakistan, Islamabad

<!-- page 3 -->

## **PREFACE** 

The Statistical Supplement is a follow up document of the Pakistan Economic Survey to provide complete data on all sectors of the economy for the entire outgoing fiscal year. It is hoped that this statistical supplement, which contains a series of data and information on socio-economic development, will be useful for policy-makers, researchers, people’s representatives and students, as well as those persons who have an interest in Pakistan’s economy.  Economic Adviser’s Wing has made concerted efforts to present time series data on financial, economic and social sectors in detail at the aggregate and sector-wise for convenience of policy makers, researchers and other users. 

I would like to thank various Ministries/Divisions/Agencies and Departments for efficiently supplying the required data to the Economic Adviser’s Wing. Without their help, it would not have been possible to release the Statistical Supplement in time. I would also like to thank my team/staff members of the Economic Adviser’s Wing for their invaluable support and hard work that enables me to complete the Statistical Supplement in time. 

We would welcome comments and suggestions for improvement of this document. Soft version of the Statistical Supplement is also available on the Website of the Finance Division. 

**Dr. Imtiaz Ahmad** Economic Adviser 

FINANCE DIVISION Islamabad, December 08, 2020 

**(i)**

## **Note:** 

**1. Total Area Reported is the total physical area of the villages/deh, tehsils or districts etc.** 

**2. Forest Area is the area of any land classed or administered as forest under any legal enactment dealing with forests. Any cultivated area which may exist within such forest is shown under heading "cultivated area".** 

**3. Area Not Available for Cultivation is that uncultivated area of the farm which is under farm home-steads, farm roads and other connected purposes and not available for cultivation.** 

**4. Culturable Waste is that uncultivated farm area which is fit for cultivation but was not cropped during the year under reference nor in the year before that.** 

**5. Current Fallow (ploughed but uncropped) is that area which is vacant during the year under reference but was sown at least once during the previous year. Cultivated Area is that area which was sown at least during the year under reference or during the previous year. Cultivated Area = Net Area sown + Current Fallow.** 

**6. Net Area Sown is that area which is sown at least once during (Kharif & Rabi) the year under reference.** 

**7. Area Sown more than once  is the difference between the total cropped area and the net area sown.** 

**8. Total Cropped Area means the aggregate area of crops raised in a farm during the year under reference including the area under fruit trees.**

## **Explanatory Notes:** 

**1. It may be noted that data series of M1 from 2000-01 is not comparable as compilation of M1 based on weekly data has been discontinued by the SBP. Now M1 is being compiled on the basis of monthly returns and as reported in the monthly Statistical Bulletin of the SBP beginning from April 2008 in its table 2.1. Now its compilation has been discontinued.** 

**2. Income velocity of money is estimated using GDP at current factor cost/ Average of quarter end monetary assets (M2).**

## **TABLE 12.5 POPULATION OF PAKISTAN BY PROVINCE, LAND AREA AND PERCENTAGE DISTRIBUTION  1951-2017** 

|**DISTRIBUTION  1951-2017**||
|---|---|

**Source: National Transport Research Center (NTRC)** 

**Note: Previously, NTRC was collecting and providing data on road length with the classification of High Type (metalled roads/ asphalt/ cement roads) and Low Type (all unmetalled roads, like shingle, earthen hard tracks). NTRC has conducted a study of Digitization of Road Directory in the country to develop a Geo-database through digitization of roads by integration of road features/ attributes. On the basis of this Digitization of Road Directory, the road length has been calculated at 501,424 km in all provinces, AJK and GB with more wide classification of Roads.**

## **WEIGHTS & MEASURES** 

||**WEIGHTS & MEASURES**|
|---|---|
|**RUPEES**<br>One Lakh<br>Ten Lakh<br>One Crore<br>One Billion<br>One Trillion<br>**WEIGHTS**|= One hundred thousand<br>= 100,000<br>= One million<br>= 1,000,000<br>= Ten million<br>= 10,000,000<br>= One thousand million<br>= One thousand billion|
|One Gram<br>One Pound<br>One Kilogram<br>One Metric ton<br>One Maund<br>One Ton<br>One cotton bale<br>One bushel<br>**LENGTH**<br>One yard<br>One mile<br>One sq. yard<br>One sq. metre<br>One Acre<br>One Hectare<br>**VOLUME**|= 0.035 Ounce<br>= 0.0857 Tola<br>= 16 ounces<br>= 453.592 grams<br>= 1000 grams<br>= 1.07 seers<br>= 2.205 pounds<br>= 1000 Kilograms<br>= 0.9842 ton<br>= 26.792 Maunds<br>= 37.3242 Kilograms<br>= 2240 pounds<br>= 1.016 metric tons<br>= 375 Ibs.<br>= 170.2 kg<br>= 0.73 mds<br>= 27.25 kg<br>= 3 feet =36 inches<br>= 0.914 metre<br>= 1760 yards<br>= 1.609 kilometres<br>= 0.83613 sq. metres<br>= 1.196 sq. yards<br>= 4840 sq. yards<br>= 0.4049 hectare<br>= 2.47 Acres|
|One cubic metre<br>**LIQUID MEASURE**<br>One barrel|= 35.315 cubic feet<br>= 36 imperial gallons<br>= 163.656 litres|



## **YEAR** 

Fiscal Year and Agriculture Year starts from 1[st] July ends on 30[th] June Before 1959-60, the fiscal year was from April 1 to March 31 

## **CROPPING SEASONS** 

**Kharif** –  Crops sown in late Spring or in the beginning of Summer and harvested in Autumn. **Rabi** –  Crops sown in Autumn and harvested in the following Spring. 

Note : Indigenous system (seers, yards etc.) and Imperial system (pound, foot etc.) in Pakistan have been replaced by International system of weights and measures (kilograms, metre etc.) w.e.f. December, 1978.
